-- Table structure for table `gmt_rating`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `gmt_rating`;
CREATE TABLE `gmt_rating` (
  `rt_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `to_user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `rt_star` float NOT NULL,
  `rt_subject` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `rt_feadback` text NOT NULL,
  `created_datetime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `created_ip` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `modified_datetime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `modified_ip` varchar(20) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `gmt_user_details`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `gmt_user_details`;
CREATE TABLE `gmt_user_details` (
  `u_detail_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `u_detail_profile_thumb_url` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `u_detail_profile_org_url` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `state_fk` varchar(60) NOT NULL,
  `district_fk` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `city` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `address1` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `address2` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `u_detail_pin` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `u_detail_pan` varchar(11) NOT NULL,
  `u_detail_tin` varchar(11) NOT NULL,
  `u_detail_stax` varchar(11) NOT NULL,
  `comp_type_id_fk` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `created_datetime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `created_ip` varchar(15) NOT NULL,
  `modified_datetime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `modified_ip` varchar(15) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
